			<!-- SoundCloud-->
<script type="rocketlazyloadscript" data-rocket-type="text/javascript" data-rocket-src="https://w.soundcloud.com/player/api.js"></script>
<script type="rocketlazyloadscript" data-rocket-type="text/javascript">
    jQuery(function(){
        var widget3 = SC.Widget("soo");
        
        var prevTrackId = "";

        jQuery(".home-top .playSound").click(function() {
            
            
            var dataId = jQuery(this).attr("data-id");

            console.log(dataId);
            
            if(dataId != prevTrackId) {
                console.log('different');
                var url = "https://api.soundcloud.com/";
                var options = [];
                // if a track 
                url += "tracks/";
                // append the id of the track / playlist to the url
                url += dataId;
                // set any options you want for the player
                options.show_artwork = false;
                options.liking = false;
                options.auto_play = true;
                options.hide_related = false;
                options.show_comments = false;
                options.show_user = false;
                options.show_reposts = false;
                options.show_teaser = false;
                options.visual = false;
                options.sharing = false;
    
                // var iframeSrc = jQuery('#so').attr('src');
                
                // console.log(iframeSrc);
                
                widget3.load(url, options);
                
                prevTrackId = dataId;
            } else {
                console.log('same');
                 widget3.toggle();
            }
            
            // console.log(url);

			if(jQuery(this).find("span").text() == "Listen") {
				jQuery(this).find("span").text('Pause');
				console.log('if');
			} else {
				jQuery(this).find("span").text('Listen');
				console.log('else');
			}  

		}); 
		
		jQuery(document).on('click', function(e) {
			var container = jQuery(".home-top-podcast");
			if (!jQuery(e.target).closest(container).length) {
				widget3.pause();
				jQuery(".playSound").find("span").text('Listen');
			}
		});
		
    });
</script>

			<!-- SoundCloud-->
<script type="rocketlazyloadscript" data-rocket-type="text/javascript" data-rocket-src="https://w.soundcloud.com/player/api.js"></script>
<script type="rocketlazyloadscript" data-rocket-type="text/javascript">
    
    jQuery(function(){
        var widget2 = SC.Widget("home-podcast");
        
        var prevTrackId = ""; 
        jQuery('body').on('click','.listen-tab-podcast .flipster__item a',function(e){
            
            e.preventDefault();
            if(jQuery(this).closest('.flipster__item').hasClass('flipster__item--current')){
                
                var href = jQuery(this).attr("href");
                var dataId = href.replace(/^https?:\/\//, '')
                console.log(dataId);
                
                if(dataId != prevTrackId) {
                    var url = "https://api.soundcloud.com/";
                    var options = [];
                    // if a track 
                    url += "tracks/";
                    // append the id of the track / playlist to the url
                    url += dataId;
                    // set any options you want for the player
                    options.show_artwork = false;
                    options.liking = false;
                    options.auto_play = true;
                    options.hide_related = false;
                    options.show_comments = false;
                    options.show_user = false;
                    options.show_reposts = false;
                    options.show_teaser = false;
                    options.visual = false;
                    options.sharing = false;
        
                    // var iframeSrc = jQuery('#so').attr('src');
                    
                    // console.log(iframeSrc);
                    
                    widget2.load(url, options);
                    
                    prevTrackId = dataId;
                } else {
                     widget2.toggle();
                }
                jQuery(this).addClass('play');
                if(jQuery(this).attr('class') == "play") {
				jQuery(this).attr('class', 'pause');
    			} else {
    				jQuery(this).attr('class', 'play');
    			}  
            }
        });
        
        jQuery(document).on('click', function(e) {
			var container = jQuery(".flipster__item--current");
			if (!jQuery(e.target).closest(container).length) {
				widget2.pause();
				jQuery('.listen-tab-podcast .flipster__item--current a').attr('class', 'play');
			}
		});
    });
</script>

				</div>
